```diff
+ import Foundation
+ import FirebaseFirestore
+ import FirebaseFirestoreSwift
+ 
+ enum NotificationType: String, Codable {
+     case userDefined = "userDefined"  // ãƒ¦ãƒ¼ã‚¶ãƒ¼ãŒè¨­å®šã—ãŸé€šçŸ¥
+     case random = "random"            // ãƒ©ãƒ³ãƒ€ãƒ ãªé€šçŸ¥
+     case urgent = "urgent"            // ç·Šæ€¥æ€§ã®é«˜ã„é€šçŸ¥
+     case gentle = "gentle"            // ã‚„ã•ã—ã„ãƒªãƒã‚¤ãƒ³ãƒ€ãƒ¼
+ }
+ 
+ enum NotificationStatus: String, Codable {
+     case scheduled = "scheduled"  // äºˆå®šæ¸ˆã¿
+     case delivered = "delivered"  // é…ä¿¡æ¸ˆã¿
+     case viewed = "viewed"        // é–²è¦§æ¸ˆã¿
+     case canceled = "canceled"    // ã‚­ãƒ£ãƒ³ã‚»ãƒ«æ¸ˆã¿
+ }
+ 
+ struct NotificationModel: Identifiable, Codable {
+     @DocumentID var id: String?
+     var userId: String
+     var taskId: String?          // é–¢é€£ã™ã‚‹ã‚¿ã‚¹ã‚¯ï¼ˆã‚ªãƒ—ã‚·ãƒ§ãƒ³ï¼‰
+     var title: String
+     var body: String
+     var type: NotificationType
+     var status: NotificationStatus
+     var scheduledDate: Date      // äºˆå®šæ—¥æ™‚
+     var deliveredDate: Date?     // é…ä¿¡æ—¥æ™‚
+     var viewedDate: Date?        // é–²è¦§æ—¥æ™‚
+     var soundEnabled: Bool = true
+     var vibrationEnabled: Bool = true
+     var characterAnimation: Bool = true  // ã‚ªã‚«ãƒ³ã®ã‚­ãƒ£ãƒ©ã‚¯ã‚¿ãƒ¼ã‚¢ãƒ‹ãƒ¡ãƒ¼ã‚·ãƒ§ãƒ³è¡¨ç¤º
+     
+     // Firebase Timestampå¤‰æ›ç”¨
+     var createdAt: Date = Date()
+     var updatedAt: Date = Date()
+     
+     // ãƒ­ãƒ¼ã‚«ãƒ«é€šçŸ¥IDï¼ˆUserNotificationsãƒ•ãƒ¬ãƒ¼ãƒ ãƒ¯ãƒ¼ã‚¯ç”¨ï¼‰
+     var localNotificationId: String?
+     
+     // Firestoreç”¨è¾æ›¸å¤‰æ›ãƒ¡ã‚½ãƒƒãƒ‰
+     func toDictionary() -> [String: Any] {
+         return [
+             "userId": userId,
+             "taskId": taskId as Any,
+             "title": title,
+             "body": body,
+             "type": type.rawValue,
+             "status": status.rawValue,
+             "scheduledDate": scheduledDate,
+             "deliveredDate": deliveredDate as Any,
+             "viewedDate": viewedDate as Any,
+             "soundEnabled": soundEnabled,
+             "vibrationEnabled": vibrationEnabled,
+             "characterAnimation": characterAnimation,
+             "createdAt": createdAt,
+             "updatedAt": updatedAt,
+             "localNotificationId": localNotificationId as Any
+         ]
+     }
+     
+     // Firestore Snapshot ã‹ã‚‰ã®åˆæœŸåŒ–
+     static func fromSnapshot(_ snapshot: DocumentSnapshot) -> NotificationModel? {
+         guard let data = snapshot.data() else { return nil }
+         
+         guard let userId = data["userId"] as? String,
+               let title = data["title"] as? String,
+               let body = data["body"] as? String,
+               let typeString = data["type"] as? String,
+               let statusString = data["status"] as? String,
+               let scheduledDate = (data["scheduledDate"] as? Timestamp)?.dateValue(),
+               let createdAt = (data["createdAt"] as? Timestamp)?.dateValue(),
+               let updatedAt = (data["updatedAt"] as? Timestamp)?.dateValue() else {
+             return nil
+         }
+         
+         let type = NotificationType(rawValue: typeString) ?? .userDefined
+         let status = NotificationStatus(rawValue: statusString) ?? .scheduled
+         
+         var model = NotificationModel(
+             id: snapshot.documentID,
+             userId: userId,
+             taskId: data["taskId"] as? String,
+             title: title,
+             body: body,
+             type: type,
+             status: status,
+             scheduledDate: scheduledDate,
+             soundEnabled: data["soundEnabled"] as? Bool ?? true,
+             vibrationEnabled: data["vibrationEnabled"] as? Bool ?? true,
+             characterAnimation: data["characterAnimation"] as? Bool ?? true,
+             createdAt: createdAt,
+             updatedAt: updatedAt
+         )
+         
+         model.deliveredDate = (data["deliveredDate"] as? Timestamp)?.dateValue()
+         model.viewedDate = (data["viewedDate"] as? Timestamp)?.dateValue()
+         model.localNotificationId = data["localNotificationId"] as? String
+         
+         return model
+     }
+ } 
+
```

```diff
+ import Foundation
+ import Firebase
+ import FirebaseFirestore
+ import FirebaseFirestoreSwift
+ import UserNotifications
+ import SwiftUI
+ import Combine
+ 
+ class NotificationService: ObservableObject {
+     
+     // ã‚·ãƒ³ã‚°ãƒ«ãƒˆãƒ³ã‚¤ãƒ³ã‚¹ã‚¿ãƒ³ã‚¹
+     static let shared = NotificationService()
+     
+     // Firestoreå‚ç…§
+     private let db = Firestore.firestore()
+     private var notificationsCollection: CollectionReference {
+         return db.collection("notifications")
+     }
+     
+     // é€šçŸ¥ã‚»ãƒ³ã‚¿ãƒ¼
+     private let notificationCenter = UNUserNotificationCenter.current()
+     
+     // å…¬é–‹ãƒ—ãƒ­ãƒ‘ãƒ†ã‚£
+     @Published var pendingNotifications: [NotificationModel] = []
+     @Published var deliveredNotifications: [NotificationModel] = []
+     @Published var hasNotificationPermission: Bool = false
+     @Published var newNotificationsCount: Int = 0
+     
+     // ãƒªã‚¹ãƒŠãƒ¼
+     private var notificationsListener: ListenerRegistration?
+     
+     // ãƒ‡ãƒ•ã‚©ãƒ«ãƒˆã®ã‚ªã‚«ãƒ³ã®ã‚»ãƒªãƒ•
+     private let defaultUrgentMessages = [
+         "ä»Šã‚„ã‚‰ãªã„ã¨ãƒã‚ºã„ã‚ˆï¼",
+         "ç· ã‚åˆ‡ã‚Šé–“è¿‘ã ã‚ˆï¼æ€¥ã„ã§ï¼",
+         "å¿˜ã‚Œã¦ãªã„ï¼Ÿé‡è¦ãªã‚¿ã‚¹ã‚¯ã‚ˆï¼",
+         "ã‚ã¨ã§ã‚„ã‚‹ã€œã¯ãƒ€ãƒ¡ï¼ä»Šã‚„ã£ã¦ï¼",
+         "ã‚ãªãŸã€ã“ã®ã¾ã¾ã˜ã‚ƒãƒ¤ãƒã„ã‚ã‚ˆï¼"
+     ]
+     
+     private let defaultGentleMessages = [
+         "ãã‚ãã‚ç¢ºèªã—ã¦ã¿ãŸã‚‰ï¼Ÿ",
+         "å…ƒæ°—ã«ã‚„ã£ã¦ã‚‹ï¼Ÿã‚¿ã‚¹ã‚¯è¦‹ã¦ã¿ã‚ˆã†ã‹",
+         "ã¡ã‚‡ã£ã¨ä¼‘æ†©ã—ãŸã‚‰ã€ã‚¿ã‚¹ã‚¯è¦‹ç›´ã—ã¦ã­",
+         "ãŠæ¯ã•ã‚“ãŒè¨€ã†ã®ã‚‚ãªã‚“ã ã‘ã©ã€è¨ˆç”»çš„ã«é€²ã‚ã‚ˆã†ã­",
+         "ã‚ãªãŸãªã‚‰ã§ãã‚‹ã‚ã€é ‘å¼µã£ã¦"
+     ]
+     
+     // åˆæœŸåŒ–
+     private init() {
+         checkNotificationPermission()
+     }
+     
+     // MARK: - é€šçŸ¥æ¨©é™
+     
+     func requestNotificationPermission() {
+         notificationCenter.requestAuthorization(options: [.alert, .sound, .badge]) { granted, error in
+             DispatchQueue.main.async {
+                 self.hasNotificationPermission = granted
+                 if granted {
+                     self.configureNotificationCategories()
+                 } else {
+                     print("é€šçŸ¥æ¨©é™ãŒæ‹’å¦ã•ã‚Œã¾ã—ãŸ: \(String(describing: error))")
+                 }
+             }
+         }
+     }
+     
+     private func checkNotificationPermission() {
+         notificationCenter.getNotificationSettings { settings in
+             DispatchQueue.main.async {
+                 self.hasNotificationPermission = settings.authorizationStatus == .authorized
+                 if self.hasNotificationPermission {
+                     self.configureNotificationCategories()
+                 }
+             }
+         }
+     }
+     
+     // é€šçŸ¥ã‚¢ã‚¯ã‚·ãƒ§ãƒ³ã®è¨­å®š
+     private func configureNotificationCategories() {
+         // ã€Œå®Œäº†ã€ã‚¢ã‚¯ã‚·ãƒ§ãƒ³
+         let completeAction = UNNotificationAction(
+             identifier: "COMPLETE_TASK",
+             title: "å®Œäº†",
+             options: .foreground
+         )
+         
+         // ã€Œå¾Œã§ã€ã‚¢ã‚¯ã‚·ãƒ§ãƒ³
+         let laterAction = UNNotificationAction(
+             identifier: "REMIND_LATER",
+             title: "ã‚ã¨ã§",
+             options: .foreground
+         )
+         
+         // ã‚¿ã‚¹ã‚¯é€šçŸ¥ç”¨ã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒª
+         let taskCategory = UNNotificationCategory(
+             identifier: "TASK_REMINDER",
+             actions: [completeAction, laterAction],
+             intentIdentifiers: [],
+             options: []
+         )
+         
+         // ã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒªã‚’ç™»éŒ²
+         notificationCenter.setNotificationCategories([taskCategory])
+     }
+     
+     // MARK: - Firestoreãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ç®¡ç†
+     
+     // ãƒ¦ãƒ¼ã‚¶ãƒ¼ã®é€šçŸ¥ãƒªã‚¹ãƒ‹ãƒ³ã‚°é–‹å§‹
+     func startListeningNotifications(for userId: String) {
+         // æ—¢å­˜ã®ãƒªã‚¹ãƒŠãƒ¼ã‚’ã‚¯ãƒªãƒ¼ãƒ³ã‚¢ãƒƒãƒ—
+         stopListeningNotifications()
+         
+         // æ–°ã—ã„ãƒªã‚¹ãƒŠãƒ¼ã‚’è¨­å®š
+         notificationsListener = notificationsCollection
+             .whereField("userId", isEqualTo: userId)
+             .order(by: "scheduledDate", descending: true)
+             .addSnapshotListener { [weak self] snapshot, error in
+                 guard let self = self else { return }
+                 
+                 if let error = error {
+                     print("é€šçŸ¥ã®ãƒªã‚¹ãƒ‹ãƒ³ã‚°ã‚¨ãƒ©ãƒ¼: \(error.localizedDescription)")
+                     return
+                 }
+                 
+                 guard let documents = snapshot?.documents else {
+                     print("é€šçŸ¥ãƒ‰ã‚­ãƒ¥ãƒ¡ãƒ³ãƒˆãŒã‚ã‚Šã¾ã›ã‚“")
+                     return
+                 }
+                 
+                 // é€šçŸ¥ãƒ¢ãƒ‡ãƒ«ã«å¤‰æ›
+                 let allNotifications = documents.compactMap { document -> NotificationModel? in
+                     return NotificationModel.fromSnapshot(document)
+                 }
+                 
+                 // ã‚¹ãƒ†ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã‚¹åˆ¥ã«ãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ«ã‚¿ãƒªãƒ³ã‚°
+                 DispatchQueue.main.async {
+                     self.pendingNotifications = allNotifications.filter { 
+                         $0.status == .scheduled 
+                     }
+                     
+                     self.deliveredNotifications = allNotifications.filter { 
+                         $0.status == .delivered || $0.status == .viewed
+                     }.sorted {
+                         $0.deliveredDate ?? $0.scheduledDate > $1.deliveredDate ?? $1.scheduledDate
+                     }
+                     
+                     // æœªèª­é€šçŸ¥ã®ã‚«ã‚¦ãƒ³ãƒˆ
+                     self.newNotificationsCount = allNotifications.filter {
+                         $0.status == .delivered && $0.viewedDate == nil
+                     }.count
+                 }
+             }
+     }
+     
+     // ãƒªã‚¹ãƒ‹ãƒ³ã‚°åœæ­¢
+     func stopListeningNotifications() {
+         notificationsListener?.remove()
+         notificationsListener = nil
+     }
+     
+     // é€šçŸ¥ã®è¿½åŠ 
+     func addNotification(_ notification: NotificationModel) async throws -> String {
+         // Firestoreã«è¿½åŠ 
+         let docRef = try await notificationsCollection.addDocument(data: notification.toDictionary())
+         
+         // ãƒ­ãƒ¼ã‚«ãƒ«é€šçŸ¥ã‚’ã‚¹ã‚±ã‚¸ãƒ¥ãƒ¼ãƒ«
+         if notification.status == .scheduled {
+             let localId = scheduleLocalNotification(notification, withId: docRef.documentID)
+             
+             // ãƒ­ãƒ¼ã‚«ãƒ«é€šçŸ¥IDã‚’æ›´æ–°
+             let update: [String: Any] = [
+                 "localNotificationId": localId,
+                 "id": docRef.documentID
+             ]
+             
+             try await docRef.updateData(update)
+         }
+         
+         return docRef.documentID
+     }
+     
+     // é€šçŸ¥ã®æ›´æ–°
+     func updateNotification(_ notification: NotificationModel) async throws {
+         guard let id = notification.id else {
+             throw NSError(domain: "NotificationService", code: 1, userInfo: [NSLocalizedDescriptionKey: "é€šçŸ¥IDãŒã‚ã‚Šã¾ã›ã‚“"])
+         }
+         
+         // Firestoreã®æ›´æ–°
+         try await notificationsCollection.document(id).updateData([
+             "title": notification.title,
+             "body": notification.body,
+             "scheduledDate": notification.scheduledDate,
+             "status": notification.status.rawValue,
+             "updatedAt": Date()
+         ])
+         
+         // æ—¢å­˜ã®ãƒ­ãƒ¼ã‚«ãƒ«é€šçŸ¥ã‚’ã‚­ãƒ£ãƒ³ã‚»ãƒ«
+         if let localId = notification.localNotificationId {
+             notificationCenter.removePendingNotificationRequests(withIdentifiers: [localId])
+         }
+         
+         // äºˆå®šã•ã‚ŒãŸé€šçŸ¥ã®å ´åˆã¯å†ã‚¹ã‚±ã‚¸ãƒ¥ãƒ¼ãƒ«
+         if notification.status == .scheduled {
+             let localId = scheduleLocalNotification(notification, withId: id)
+             
+             // ãƒ­ãƒ¼ã‚«ãƒ«é€šçŸ¥IDã‚’æ›´æ–°
+             try await notificationsCollection.document(id).updateData([
+                 "localNotificationId": localId
+             ])
+         }
+     }
+     
+     // é€šçŸ¥ã‚’æ—¢èª­ã«è¨­å®š
+     func markNotificationAsViewed(_ notification: NotificationModel) async throws {
+         guard let id = notification.id else { return }
+         
+         var updatedNotification = notification
+         updatedNotification.status = .viewed
+         updatedNotification.viewedDate = Date()
+         
+         try await notificationsCollection.document(id).updateData([
+             "status": NotificationStatus.viewed.rawValue,
+             "viewedDate": Date(),
+             "updatedAt": Date()
+         ])
+     }
+     
+     // é€šçŸ¥ã®å‰Šé™¤
+     func deleteNotification(_ notification: NotificationModel) async throws {
+         guard let id = notification.id else { return }
+         
+         // ãƒ­ãƒ¼ã‚«ãƒ«é€šçŸ¥ã‚’ã‚­ãƒ£ãƒ³ã‚»ãƒ«
+         if let localId = notification.localNotificationId {
+             notificationCenter.removePendingNotificationRequests(withIdentifiers: [localId])
+         }
+         
+         // Firestoreã‹ã‚‰å‰Šé™¤
+         try await notificationsCollection.document(id).delete()
+     }
+     
+     // MARK: - ãƒ­ãƒ¼ã‚«ãƒ«é€šçŸ¥ç®¡ç†
+     
+     // ãƒ­ãƒ¼ã‚«ãƒ«é€šçŸ¥ã‚’ã‚¹ã‚±ã‚¸ãƒ¥ãƒ¼ãƒ«
+     private func scheduleLocalNotification(_ notification: NotificationModel, withId id: String) -> String {
+         let content = UNMutableNotificationContent()
+         content.title = notification.title
+         content.body = notification.body
+         content.sound = notification.soundEnabled ? .default : nil
+         
+         // ã‚¢ã‚¯ã‚·ãƒ§ãƒ³ã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒªã®è¨­å®š
+         if notification.taskId != nil {
+             content.categoryIdentifier = "TASK_REMINDER"
+         }
+         
+         // é€šçŸ¥ã®ã‚«ã‚¹ã‚¿ãƒ ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿
+         content.userInfo = [
+             "notificationId": id,
+             "taskId": notification.taskId as Any,
+             "type": notification.type.rawValue
+         ]
+         
+         // é€šçŸ¥ãƒˆãƒªã‚¬ãƒ¼ã®ä½œæˆ
+         let trigger = UNTimeIntervalNotificationTrigger(
+             timeInterval: max(1, notification.scheduledDate.timeIntervalSinceNow),
+             repeats: false
+         )
+         
+         // ãƒ­ãƒ¼ã‚«ãƒ«é€šçŸ¥ã®IDç”Ÿæˆ
+         let localId = UUID().uuidString
+         
+         // é€šçŸ¥ãƒªã‚¯ã‚¨ã‚¹ãƒˆã®ä½œæˆ
+         let request = UNNotificationRequest(
+             identifier: localId,
+             content: content,
+             trigger: trigger
+         )
+         
+         // é€šçŸ¥ã®ã‚¹ã‚±ã‚¸ãƒ¥ãƒ¼ãƒ«
+         notificationCenter.add(request) { error in
+             if let error = error {
+                 print("ãƒ­ãƒ¼ã‚«ãƒ«é€šçŸ¥ã®ã‚¹ã‚±ã‚¸ãƒ¥ãƒ¼ãƒ«ã‚¨ãƒ©ãƒ¼: \(error.localizedDescription)")
+             }
+         }
+         
+         return localId
+     }
+     
+     // ä¿ç•™ä¸­ã®ãƒ­ãƒ¼ã‚«ãƒ«é€šçŸ¥ã‚’å–å¾—
+     func getPendingLocalNotifications() async -> [UNNotificationRequest] {
+         do {
+             return try await notificationCenter.pendingNotificationRequests()
+         } catch {
+             print("ä¿ç•™ä¸­ã®é€šçŸ¥å–å¾—ã‚¨ãƒ©ãƒ¼: \(error.localizedDescription)")
+             return []
+         }
+     }
+     
+     // é…ä¿¡æ¸ˆã¿ãƒ­ãƒ¼ã‚«ãƒ«é€šçŸ¥ã‚’å–å¾—
+     func getDeliveredLocalNotifications() async -> [UNNotification] {
+         do {
+             return try await notificationCenter.deliveredNotifications()
+         } catch {
+             print("é…ä¿¡æ¸ˆã¿é€šçŸ¥å–å¾—ã‚¨ãƒ©ãƒ¼: \(error.localizedDescription)")
+             return []
+         }
+     }
+     
+     // MARK: - ãƒ¦ãƒ¼ãƒ†ã‚£ãƒªãƒ†ã‚£ãƒ¡ã‚½ãƒƒãƒ‰
+     
+     // ã‚¿ã‚¹ã‚¯ã‹ã‚‰ãƒªãƒã‚¤ãƒ³ãƒ€ãƒ¼é€šçŸ¥ã‚’ä½œæˆ
+     func createTaskReminderNotification(for task: Task, userId: String, type: NotificationType, scheduledDate: Date) -> NotificationModel {
+         var title = "ã‚¿ã‚¹ã‚¯ãƒªãƒã‚¤ãƒ³ãƒ€ãƒ¼"
+         var body = task.title
+         
+         // é€šçŸ¥ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒ—ã«å¿œã˜ãŸãƒ¡ãƒƒã‚»ãƒ¼ã‚¸
+         switch type {
+         case .urgent:
+             title = "æ€¥ã„ã§ï¼"
+             body = "\(task.title) - \(defaultUrgentMessages.randomElement() ?? "ä»Šã™ãç¢ºèªã—ã¦ï¼")"
+         case .gentle:
+             title = "ãŠæ¯ã•ã‚“ã‚ˆã‚Š"
+             body = "\(task.title) - \(defaultGentleMessages.randomElement() ?? "ãã‚ãã‚ç¢ºèªã—ã¦ã­")"
+         default:
+             title = "ãƒªãƒã‚¤ãƒ³ãƒ€ãƒ¼"
+             body = task.title
+         }
+         
+         return NotificationModel(
+             userId: userId,
+             taskId: task.id,
+             title: title,
+             body: body,
+             type: type,
+             status: .scheduled,
+             scheduledDate: scheduledDate
+         )
+     }
+     
+     // ãƒ©ãƒ³ãƒ€ãƒ é€šçŸ¥ã‚’ä½œæˆï¼ˆAIã‚ªã‚«ãƒ³ã‹ã‚‰ã®çªç™ºçš„ãªé€šçŸ¥ï¼‰
+     func createRandomNotification(for userId: String, withTasks tasks: [Task]? = nil) -> NotificationModel? {
+         // ã‚¿ã‚¹ã‚¯ãŒå­˜åœ¨ã™ã‚‹å ´åˆã¯ãƒ©ãƒ³ãƒ€ãƒ ã«é¸æŠ
+         let task = tasks?.randomElement()
+         
+         // é€šçŸ¥ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒ—ã‚’ãƒ©ãƒ³ãƒ€ãƒ ã«é¸æŠï¼ˆç·Šæ€¥ã¾ãŸã¯ã‚„ã•ã—ã„ï¼‰
+         let type: NotificationType = Bool.random() ? .urgent : .gentle
+         
+         var title = type == .urgent ? "æ€¥ã„ã§ï¼" : "ãŠæ¯ã•ã‚“ã‚ˆã‚Š"
+         var body = ""
+         
+         if let selectedTask = task {
+             // ã‚¿ã‚¹ã‚¯ãŒé¸æŠã•ã‚ŒãŸå ´åˆ
+             body = type == .urgent 
+                 ? "\(selectedTask.title) - \(defaultUrgentMessages.randomElement() ?? "ä»Šã™ãç¢ºèªã—ã¦ï¼")"
+                 : "\(selectedTask.title) - \(defaultGentleMessages.randomElement() ?? "ãã‚ãã‚ç¢ºèªã—ã¦ã­")"
+         } else {
+             // ã‚¿ã‚¹ã‚¯ãŒãªã„å ´åˆã®ä¸€èˆ¬çš„ãªãƒ¡ãƒƒã‚»ãƒ¼ã‚¸
+             body = type == .urgent
+                 ? defaultUrgentMessages.randomElement() ?? "ã‚¿ã‚¹ã‚¯ã‚’ç¢ºèªã—ã¦ï¼"
+                 : defaultGentleMessages.randomElement() ?? "å…ƒæ°—ã«ã—ã¦ã‚‹ï¼Ÿ"
+         }
+         
+         // é€šçŸ¥ã®ä½œæˆ
+         return NotificationModel(
+             userId: userId,
+             taskId: task?.id,
+             title: title,
+             body: body,
+             type: type,
+             status: .scheduled,
+             scheduledDate: Date()
+         )
+     }
+     
+     // é€šçŸ¥ãƒãƒƒã‚¸ã‚’ã‚¯ãƒªã‚¢
+     func clearNotificationBadge() {
+         UNUserNotificationCenter.current().setBadgeCount(0) { error in
+             if let error = error {
+                 print("ãƒãƒƒã‚¸ã‚¯ãƒªã‚¢ã‚¨ãƒ©ãƒ¼: \(error.localizedDescription)")
+             }
+         }
+     }
+ } 
+ 
```

```diff
+ struct NotificationSettingsView: View {

+     @StateObject private var notificationService = NotificationService.shared

+     @State private var isCharacterEnabled = true
+     @State private var showingPermissionAlert = false
+     
+     var body: some View {
+         List {
+             Section(header: Text("é€šçŸ¥")) {
+                 Toggle("ã‚¿ã‚¹ã‚¯ãƒªãƒã‚¤ãƒ³ãƒ€ãƒ¼", isOn: $isTaskRemindersEnabled)
+                     .onChange(of: isTaskRemindersEnabled) { newValue in
+                         if newValue && !notificationService.hasNotificationPermission {
+                             showingPermissionAlert = true
+                         }
+                         updateUserSettings()
+                     }
+                 
+                 Toggle("ãƒ©ãƒ³ãƒ€ãƒ ãƒªãƒã‚¤ãƒ³ãƒ€ãƒ¼ï¼ˆAIã‚ªã‚«ãƒ³ï¼‰", isOn: $isRandomRemindersEnabled)

+             }

+             Section(header: Text("é€šçŸ¥ã‚¹ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒ«")) {
+                 Toggle("ã‚µã‚¦ãƒ³ãƒ‰", isOn: $isSoundEnabled)
+                     .onChange(of: isSoundEnabled) { _ in updateUserSettings() }
+                 
+                 Toggle("ãƒã‚¤ãƒ–ãƒ¬ãƒ¼ã‚·ãƒ§ãƒ³", isOn: $isVibrationEnabled)
+                     .onChange(of: isVibrationEnabled) { _ in updateUserSettings() }
+                 
+                 Toggle("ã‚ªã‚«ãƒ³ã‚­ãƒ£ãƒ©ã‚¯ã‚¿ãƒ¼è¡¨ç¤º", isOn: $isCharacterEnabled)
+                     .onChange(of: isCharacterEnabled) { _ in updateUserSettings() }
+             }
+             
+             Section {
+                 Button(action: {
+                     notificationService.requestNotificationPermission()
+                 }) {
+                     HStack {
+                         Text("é€šçŸ¥æ¨©é™ã‚’ç¢ºèª")
+                         Spacer()

+                             .foregroundColor(notificationService.hasNotificationPermission ? .green : .red)
+                     }
+                 }
+             }
+         }

+         .onAppear {
+             loadUserSettings()
+         }

+             Alert(
+                 title: Text("é€šçŸ¥æ¨©é™ãŒå¿…è¦ã§ã™"),
+                 message: Text("ã“ã®æ©Ÿèƒ½ã‚’ä½¿ç”¨ã™ã‚‹ã«ã¯é€šçŸ¥æ¨©é™ãŒå¿…è¦ã§ã™ã€‚è¨­å®šã‚¢ãƒ—ãƒªã‹ã‚‰è¨±å¯ã—ã¦ãã ã•ã„ã€‚"),
+                 primaryButton: .default(Text("è¨­å®šã‚’é–‹ã"), action: {
+                     if let url = URL(string: UIApplication.openSettingsURLString) {
+                         UIApplication.shared.open(url)
+                     }
+                 }),
+                 secondaryButton: .cancel(Text("ã‚­ãƒ£ãƒ³ã‚»ãƒ«"))
+             )
+         }
+     }
+     
+     private func loadUserSettings() {
+         guard let currentUser = userService.currentUser else { return }
+         
+         isTaskRemindersEnabled = currentUser.notificationPreferences?.enableTaskReminders ?? true
+         isRandomRemindersEnabled = currentUser.notificationPreferences?.enableRandomReminders ?? true
+         isSoundEnabled = currentUser.notificationPreferences?.enableSound ?? true
+         isVibrationEnabled = currentUser.notificationPreferences?.enableVibration ?? true
+         isCharacterEnabled = currentUser.notificationPreferences?.enableCharacterAnimation ?? true
+     }
+     
+     private func updateUserSettings() {
+         guard var currentUser = userService.currentUser else { return }
+         
+         let preferences = NotificationPreferences(
+             enableTaskReminders: isTaskRemindersEnabled,
+             enableRandomReminders: isRandomRemindersEnabled,
+             enableSound: isSoundEnabled,
+             enableVibration: isVibrationEnabled,
+             enableCharacterAnimation: isCharacterEnabled
+         )
+         
+         currentUser.notificationPreferences = preferences
+         
+         Task {
+             do {
+                 try await userService.updateUser(currentUser)
+             } catch {
+                 print("ãƒ¦ãƒ¼ã‚¶ãƒ¼è¨­å®šã®æ›´æ–°ã‚¨ãƒ©ãƒ¼: \(error.localizedDescription)")
+             }
+         }
+     }
+ }
+ 
+ struct NotificationPreferences: Codable {
+     var enableTaskReminders: Bool = true
+     var enableRandomReminders: Bool = true
+     var enableSound: Bool = true
+     var enableVibration: Bool = true
+     var enableCharacterAnimation: Bool = true
+ }
+
```

```diff
+ struct NotificationsListView: View {
+     @EnvironmentObject private var userService: UserService
+     @StateObject private var notificationService = NotificationService.shared

+     @State private var showingPermissionAlert = false

+                             Button(role: .destructive) {

+                                     try await notificationService.deleteNotification(notification)
+                                 }

+                                 Label("å‰Šé™¤", systemImage: "trash")
+                             }
+                             
+                             if notification.status == .delivered {
+                                 Button {
+                                     Task {
+                                         try await notificationService.markNotificationAsViewed(notification)
+                                     }
+                                 } label: {
+                                     Label("æ—¢èª­", systemImage: "checkmark")
+                                 }
+                                 .tint(.blue)
+                             }
+                         }
+                         .onAppear {
+                             // é€šçŸ¥ã‚’æ—¢èª­ã«ã™ã‚‹
+                             if notification.status == .delivered {
+                                 Task {
+                                     try await notificationService.markNotificationAsViewed(notification)
+                                 }
+                             }
+                         }
+                 }
+             }
+         }
+         .listStyle(InsetGroupedListStyle())
+         .animation(.default, value: notificationService.deliveredNotifications)
+     }
+     
+     private var pendingNotificationsList: some View {
+         List {
+             if notificationService.pendingNotifications.isEmpty {
+                 Text("äºˆå®šã•ã‚ŒãŸé€šçŸ¥ã¯ã‚ã‚Šã¾ã›ã‚“")
+                     .foregroundColor(.gray)
+                     .frame(maxWidth: .infinity, alignment: .center)
+                     .padding()
+             } else {
+                 ForEach(notificationService.pendingNotifications) { notification in
+                     NotificationRowView(notification: notification)
+                         .swipeActions {
+                             Button(role: .destructive) {
+                                 Task {
+                                     try await notificationService.deleteNotification(notification)
+                                 }
+                             } label: {
+                                 Label("ã‚­ãƒ£ãƒ³ã‚»ãƒ«", systemImage: "xmark.circle")
+                             }
+                         }
+                 }
+             }
+         }
+         .listStyle(InsetGroupedListStyle())
+         .animation(.default, value: notificationService.pendingNotifications)
+     }
+     
+     private func setupNotifications() {
+         guard let userId = userService.currentUser?.id else { return }
+         
+         // é€šçŸ¥ãƒªã‚¹ãƒŠãƒ¼ã‚’é–‹å§‹
+         notificationService.startListeningNotifications(for: userId)
+         
+         // é€šçŸ¥ãƒãƒƒã‚¸ã‚’ã‚¯ãƒªã‚¢
+         notificationService.clearNotificationBadge()
+     }
+ }
+ 
+ struct NotificationRowView: View {
+     let notification: NotificationModel
+     
+     private var typeIcon: String {
+         switch notification.type {
+         case .urgent: return "exclamationmark.triangle.fill"
+         case .gentle: return "heart.fill"
+         case .userDefined: return "bell.fill"
+         case .random: return "sparkles"
+         }
+     }
+     
+     private var typeColor: Color {
+         switch notification.type {
+         case .urgent: return .red
+         case .gentle: return .blue
+         case .userDefined: return .green
+         case .random: return .purple
+         }
+     }
+     
+     private var formattedDate: String {
+         let formatter = DateFormatter()
+         formatter.dateStyle = .short
+         formatter.timeStyle = .short
+         formatter.locale = Locale(identifier: "ja_JP")
+         
+         if notification.status == .delivered || notification.status == .viewed {
+             return formatter.string(from: notification.deliveredDate ?? notification.scheduledDate)
+         } else {
+             return formatter.string(from: notification.scheduledDate)
+         }
+     }
+     
+     var body: some View {
+         HStack(alignment: .top, spacing: 12) {
+             Image(systemName: typeIcon)
+                 .foregroundColor(typeColor)
+                 .font(.title2)
+                 .frame(width: 24, height: 24)
+             
+             VStack(alignment: .leading, spacing: 4) {
+                 Text(notification.title)
+                     .font(.headline)
+                     .foregroundColor(notification.status == .viewed ? .gray : .primary)
+                 
+                 Text(notification.body)
+                     .font(.subheadline)
+                     .foregroundColor(.secondary)
+                     .lineLimit(2)
+                 
+                 Text(formattedDate)
+                     .font(.caption)
+                     .foregroundColor(.gray)
+             }
+             
+             Spacer()
+             
+             if notification.status == .delivered {
+                 Circle()
+                     .fill(Color.blue)
+                     .frame(width: 10, height: 10)
+             }
+         }
+         .padding(.vertical, 8)
+     }
+ }
+ 
+ struct NotificationsListView_Previews: PreviewProvider {
+     static var previews: some View {
+         NavigationView {
+             NotificationsListView()
+                 .environmentObject(UserService.shared)
+         }
+     }
+ } 
+ 
```

```swift
func updateUser(_ userProfile: UserProfile) async throws {
    return try await withCheckedThrowingContinuation { continuation in
        updateUserProfile(userProfile: userProfile)
            .sink(receiveCompletion: { completion in
                switch completion {
                case .finished:
                    break
                case .failure(let error):
                    continuation.resume(throwing: error)
                }
            }, receiveValue: { updatedProfile in
                DispatchQueue.main.async {
                    self.currentUserProfile = updatedProfile
                }
                continuation.resume(returning: ())
            })
            .store(in: &self.cancellables)
    }
}
```

```swift
private func updateUserSettings() {
    guard var currentUser = userService.currentUserProfile else { return }
    
    let preferences = NotificationPreferences(
        enableTaskReminders: isTaskRemindersEnabled,
        enableRandomReminders: isRandomRemindersEnabled,
        enableSound: isSoundEnabled,
        enableVibration: isVibrationEnabled,
        enableCharacterAnimation: isCharacterEnabled
    )
    
    currentUser.notificationPreferences = preferences
    
    Task {
        do {
            try await userService.updateUser(currentUser)
        } catch {
            print("ãƒ¦ãƒ¼ã‚¶ãƒ¼è¨­å®šã®æ›´æ–°ã‚¨ãƒ©ãƒ¼: \(error.localizedDescription)")
        }
    }
}
```

æœ€æ–°ã®Swiftæ§‹æ–‡ã§ã¯ã€Taskãƒ–ãƒ­ãƒƒã‚¯ã®ä¸­ã§awaitã‚’ä½¿ã†éš›ã«æ§‹æ–‡ãŒå¤‰ã‚ã£ãŸã“ã¨ãŒã‚ã‚Šã¾ã™ã€‚ã‚‚ã—ãã¯ã€SwiftUIã®Viewã®ä¸­ã§Taskã‚’ç›´æ¥ä½¿ã†æ–¹æ³•ã«å•é¡ŒãŒã‚ã‚‹ã‹ã‚‚ã—ã‚Œã¾ã›ã‚“ã€‚

ä¿®æ­£æ¡ˆã¨ã—ã¦ã¯ï¼š

ã¾ãšã¯1ç•ªã®æ–¹æ³•ã‚’è©¦ã—ã¦ã¿ã¾ã—ã‚‡ã†ã€‚

```diff
- struct NotificationModel: Identifiable, Codable {
+ struct NotificationModel: Identifiable, Codable, Equatable {
      @DocumentID var id: String?
      var userId: String
          return model
      }
+     
+     // Equatableãƒ—ãƒ­ãƒˆã‚³ãƒ«æº–æ‹ ã®ãŸã‚ã®å®Ÿè£…
+     static func == (lhs: NotificationModel, rhs: NotificationModel) -> Bool {
+         return lhs.id == rhs.id &&
+                lhs.userId == rhs.userId &&
+                lhs.taskId == rhs.taskId &&
+                lhs.title == rhs.title &&
+                lhs.body == rhs.body &&
+                lhs.type == rhs.type &&
+                lhs.status == rhs.status &&
+                lhs.scheduledDate == rhs.scheduledDate &&
+                lhs.deliveredDate == rhs.deliveredDate &&
+                lhs.viewedDate == rhs.viewedDate &&
+                lhs.soundEnabled == rhs.soundEnabled &&
+                lhs.vibrationEnabled == rhs.vibrationEnabled &&
+                lhs.characterAnimation == rhs.characterAnimation
+     }
  }
```

```diff
- 
+ import SwiftUI
+ 
+ struct NotificationRowView: View {
+     let notification: NotificationModel
+     
+     private var typeIcon: String {
+         switch notification.type {
+         case .urgent: return "exclamationmark.triangle.fill"
+         case .gentle: return "heart.fill"
+         case .userDefined: return "bell.fill"
+         case .random: return "sparkles"
+         }
+     }
+     
+     private var typeColor: Color {
+         switch notification.type {
+         case .urgent: return .red
+         case .gentle: return .blue
+         case .userDefined: return .green
+         case .random: return .purple
+         }
+     }
+     
+     private var formattedDate: String {
+         let formatter = DateFormatter()
+         formatter.dateStyle = .short
+         formatter.timeStyle = .short
+         formatter.locale = Locale(identifier: "ja_JP")
+         
+         if notification.status == .delivered || notification.status == .viewed {
+             return formatter.string(from: notification.deliveredDate ?? notification.scheduledDate)
+         } else {
+             return formatter.string(from: notification.scheduledDate)
+         }
+     }
+     
+     var body: some View {
+         HStack(alignment: .top, spacing: 12) {
+             Image(systemName: typeIcon)
+                 .foregroundColor(typeColor)
+                 .font(.title2)
+                 .frame(width: 24, height: 24)
+             
+             VStack(alignment: .leading, spacing: 4) {
+                 Text(notification.title)
+                     .font(.headline)
+                     .foregroundColor(notification.status == .viewed ? .gray : .primary)
+                 
+                 Text(notification.body)
+                     .font(.subheadline)
+                     .foregroundColor(.secondary)
+                     .lineLimit(2)
+                 
+                 Text(formattedDate)
+                     .font(.caption)
+                     .foregroundColor(.gray)
+             }
+             
+             Spacer()
+             
+             if notification.status == .delivered {
+                 Circle()
+                     .fill(Color.blue)
+                     .frame(width: 10, height: 10)
+             }
+         }
+         .padding(.vertical, 8)
+     }
+ } 
+ 
```

```swift:AIokan/Views/Notifications/NotificationsListView.swift
    NavigationLink(destination: NotificationSettingsView()) {
        Text("é€šçŸ¥è¨­å®š")
    }
    
    Button("ãƒ†ã‚¹ãƒˆãƒãƒŠãƒ¼é€šçŸ¥ã‚’é€ä¿¡") {
        let content = UNMutableNotificationContent()
        content.title = "ãƒ†ã‚¹ãƒˆé€šçŸ¥"
        content.body = "ã“ã‚Œã¯ãƒãƒŠãƒ¼é€šçŸ¥ã®ãƒ†ã‚¹ãƒˆã§ã™"
        content.sound = .default

            if let error = error {
                print("ãƒ†ã‚¹ãƒˆé€šçŸ¥ã®é€ä¿¡ã«å¤±æ•—: \(error)")

            }
```

```diff
+             let taskData = newTask.toFirestore()
+             
+             // Firestoreã«è¿½åŠ 
+             var ref: DocumentReference? = nil
+             ref = self.db.collection(self.tasksCollection).addDocument(data: taskData) { error in
+                 if let error = error {
+                     print("ã‚¿ã‚¹ã‚¯ä½œæˆã‚¨ãƒ©ãƒ¼: \(error.localizedDescription)")
+                     promise(.failure(error))
+                     return
+                 }
+                 
+                 guard let id = ref?.documentID else {
+                     promise(.failure(NSError(domain: "TaskService", code: -1, userInfo: [NSLocalizedDescriptionKey: "ã‚¿ã‚¹ã‚¯IDã®å–å¾—ã«å¤±æ•—ã—ã¾ã—ãŸ"])))
+                     return
+                 }
+                 
+                 print("ã‚¿ã‚¹ã‚¯ä½œæˆæˆåŠŸ: \(id)")
+                 
+                 // IDã‚’è¨­å®šã—ã¦è¿”ã™
+                 newTask.id = id
+                 
+                 // ã‚¿ã‚¹ã‚¯ä½œæˆæˆåŠŸå¾Œã€é€šçŸ¥ã‚’ã‚¹ã‚±ã‚¸ãƒ¥ãƒ¼ãƒ«
+                 self.notificationService.scheduleTaskNotification(for: newTask, userId: userId)
+                 print("ğŸ”” ã‚¿ã‚¹ã‚¯é€šçŸ¥ãŒã‚¹ã‚±ã‚¸ãƒ¥ãƒ¼ãƒ«ã•ã‚Œã¾ã—ãŸ: \(id)")
+                 
+                 promise(.success(newTask))
+             }
          }
          .eraseToAnyPublisher()
```

```diff
+     func startListeningNotifications(for userId: String) {
+         // æ—¢å­˜ã®ãƒªã‚¹ãƒŠãƒ¼ãŒã‚ã‚Œã°å‰Šé™¤
+         notificationsListener?.remove()
+         
+         // Firestoreã‹ã‚‰é€šçŸ¥ã‚’å–å¾—ã™ã‚‹ãƒªã‚¹ãƒŠãƒ¼ã‚’è¨­å®š
+         notificationsListener = db.collection("notifications")
+             .whereField("userId", isEqualTo: userId)
+             .order(by: "scheduledDate", descending: true)
+             .addSnapshotListener { [weak self] snapshot, error in
+                 guard let self = self else { return }
+                 
+                 if let error = error {
+                     print("é€šçŸ¥ãƒªã‚¹ãƒŠãƒ¼ã‚¨ãƒ©ãƒ¼: \(error.localizedDescription)")
+                     return
+                 }
+                 
+                 guard let documents = snapshot?.documents else {
+                     print("é€šçŸ¥ãƒ‰ã‚­ãƒ¥ãƒ¡ãƒ³ãƒˆãŒå­˜åœ¨ã—ã¾ã›ã‚“")
+                     return
+                 }
+                 
+                 // é€šçŸ¥ãƒ¢ãƒ‡ãƒ«ã«å¤‰æ›
+                 let notifications = documents.compactMap { document -> NotificationModel? in
+                     var notification = try? document.data(as: NotificationModel.self)
+                     notification?.id = document.documentID
+                     return notification
+                 }
+                 
+                 // é…ä¿¡æ¸ˆã¿ã¨ä¿ç•™ä¸­ã®é€šçŸ¥ã‚’åˆ†é¡
+                 DispatchQueue.main.async {
+                     self.pendingNotifications = notifications.filter { $0.status == .scheduled }
+                     self.deliveredNotifications = notifications.filter { $0.status == .delivered || $0.status == .viewed }
+                     
+                     // æœªèª­ã®é€šçŸ¥æ•°ã‚’ã‚«ã‚¦ãƒ³ãƒˆ
+                     self.newNotificationsCount = notifications.filter { $0.status == .delivered }.count
+                 }
+             }
+     }
  } 
  
```

```diff
+         switch reminderType {
+         case .urgent:
+             return .urgent
+         case .gentle:
```
